## å¤šç»´æ•°ç»„

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šå¤šç»´æ•°ç»„æ˜¯æ•°ç»„çš„æ•°ç»„ï¼Œç”¨äºå­˜å‚¨è¡¨æ ¼ã€çŸ©é˜µç­‰å¤šç»´æ•°æ®ç»“æ„ã€‚ç›¸æ¯”å•ç»´æ•°ç»„ï¼Œå¤šç»´æ•°ç»„çš„æ‰“å°å’Œè®¿é—®éœ€è¦ç‰¹æ®Šå¤„ç†ã€‚

## è¿ç®—ç¬¦ä¼˜å…ˆçº§

## ç±»å‹è½¬æ¢ä¸å¼ºåˆ¶è½¬æ¢

## Math ç±»ä¸æ•°å­¦è¿ç®—

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šMath ç±»æä¾›ä¸€ç³»åˆ—æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œç”¨äºæ‰§è¡Œå¸¸è§çš„æ•°å­¦è¿ç®—ï¼Œå¦‚å–æ•´ã€æ¯”è¾ƒå’Œéšæœºæ•°ç”Ÿæˆã€‚å®ƒç®€åŒ–äº†æ•°å­¦è®¡ç®—æ“ä½œï¼Œå¹¶ç¡®ä¿ä»£ç ç®€æ´ã€æ˜“äºç»´æŠ¤ã€‚

    - randomï¼šç”Ÿæˆ 0.0 è‡³ 1.0 ä¹‹é—´çš„éšæœº double æ•°ï¼Œæ¯æ¬¡è°ƒç”¨å¯èƒ½ä¸åŒ

3. ç±»å‹è½¬æ¢æ³¨æ„

    - è¿”å›å€¼åŒ¹é…ï¼šç¡®ä¿å˜é‡ç±»å‹ä¸æ–¹æ³•è¿”å›ç±»å‹ä¸€è‡´ï¼Œå¿…è¦æ—¶è¿›è¡Œæ˜¾å¼è½¬æ¢
    - è¡¨è¾¾å¼é¡ºåºï¼šä½¿ç”¨æ‹¬å·ç¡®ä¿è¿ç®—é¡ºåºæ­£ç¡®ï¼Œé¿å…éšå¼è½¬æ¢é”™è¯¯

**ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹**

1. å–æ•´ç¤ºä¾‹

    ```java

    int roundResult = (int) Math.round(d); // å››èˆäº”å…¥ï¼š3.7 â†’ 4
    int ceilResult = (int) Math.ceil(d);     // å‘ä¸Šå–æ•´ï¼š3.7 â†’ 4
    int floorResult = (int) Math.floor(d);   // å‘ä¸‹å–æ•´ï¼š3.7 â†’ 3
    System.out.println(roundResult);
    System.out.println(ceilResult);
    System.out.println(floorResult);
    ```

2. æ¯”è¾ƒä¸éšæœºæ•°ç¤ºä¾‹

    ```java
    int a = 10, b = 20;
    int maxVal = Math.max(a, b);   // è¿”å›è¾ƒå¤§å€¼ï¼š20
    int minVal = Math.min(a, b);   // è¿”å›è¾ƒå°å€¼ï¼š10
    double randomVal = Math.random(); // ç”Ÿæˆ 0.0 ~ 1.0 çš„éšæœºæ•°
    System.out.println(maxVal);
    System.out.println(minVal);
    System.out.println(randomVal);
    ```

3. ç”Ÿæˆ 0-100 éšæœºæ•°

    ```java

    int randomVal = (int) (Math.random() * 100);

    ```

## æ•°å­—æ ¼å¼åŒ–

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šæ•°å­—æ ¼å¼åŒ–ç”¨äºå°†æ•°å€¼è½¬æ¢ä¸ºç¬¦åˆç‰¹å®šæ ¼å¼çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œå¦‚è´§å¸å’Œç™¾åˆ†æ¯”æ˜¾ç¤ºã€‚é€šè¿‡ NumberFormat ç±»çš„å·¥å‚æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œå¯ä»¥è½»æ¾è·å–ç›¸åº”å®ä¾‹å¹¶è°ƒç”¨æ ¼å¼åŒ–æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œæ»¡è¶³ä¸åŒåœºæ™¯çš„æ˜¾ç¤ºéœ€æ±‚ã€‚

**çŸ¥è¯†æ ‘**

1. NumberFormat ç±»æ¦‚è¿°

    - å®šä¹‰ï¼šä½äº java.text åŒ…çš„æŠ½è±¡ç±»ï¼Œç”¨äºæ ¼å¼åŒ–å’Œè§£ææ•°å­—
    - ç‰¹ç‚¹ï¼šæŠ½è±¡ç±»ä¸èƒ½ç›´æ¥å®ä¾‹åŒ–ï¼Œéœ€è¦é€šè¿‡å®ƒçš„å·¥å‚æ–¹æ³•è·å–å®ä¾‹
    - æŠ½è±¡å°†åœ¨åç»­è¯¾ç¨‹è®²è§£ï¼Œè¿™é‡Œåªéœ€è®°ä½ï¼ŒæŠ½è±¡ç±»ä¸èƒ½ç›´æ¥åˆ›å»ºå®ä¾‹

2. è´§å¸æ ¼å¼åŒ–

    - å·¥å‚æ–¹æ³•ï¼š`getCurrencyInstance()` è¿”å›è´§å¸æ ¼å¼åŒ–å®ä¾‹
    - æ ¼å¼åŒ–æ–¹æ³•ï¼š`format(æ•°å­—)` å°†æ•°å€¼è½¬æ¢ä¸ºå¸¦è´§å¸ç¬¦å·å’Œåˆ†éš”ç¬¦çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²

3. ç™¾åˆ†æ¯”æ ¼å¼åŒ–

    - å·¥å‚æ–¹æ³•ï¼š`getPercentInstance()` è¿”å›ç™¾åˆ†æ¯”æ ¼å¼åŒ–å®ä¾‹
    - æ ¼å¼åŒ–æ–¹æ³•ï¼š`format(æ•°å­—)` å°†æ•°å€¼è½¬æ¢ä¸ºå¸¦ç™¾åˆ†å·çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²

    - æ–¹æ³•é“¾ï¼šå¯ç›´æ¥è°ƒç”¨å·¥å‚æ–¹æ³•åé“¾å¼è°ƒç”¨ `format()`ï¼Œç®€åŒ–ä»£ç 

**ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹**

1. è´§å¸æ ¼å¼åŒ–ç¤ºä¾‹

    ```java

    ```

2. ç™¾åˆ†æ¯”æ ¼å¼åŒ–ä¸æ–¹æ³•é“¾

    ```java

    // é“¾å¼ç¼–ç¨‹
    ```

## ç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥ä¸ Scanner

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šScanner ç±»ç”¨äºè¯»å–ç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥æ•°æ®ï¼Œå¯æŒ‡å®šè¾“å…¥æºï¼ˆå¦‚ç»ˆç«¯ã€æ–‡ä»¶ç­‰ï¼‰ï¼Œå¹¶æä¾›å¤šç§è¯»å–æ–¹æ³•ï¼ˆå¦‚ next()ã€nextLine()ã€nextInt() ç­‰ï¼‰æ¥è·å–ä¸åŒç±»å‹çš„æ•°æ®ï¼ŒåŒæ—¶å¯åˆ©ç”¨ trim() æ–¹æ³•æ¸…ç†å¤šä½™ç©ºç™½ã€‚

**çŸ¥è¯†æ ‘**

1. Scanner ç±»æ¦‚è¿°

    - å®šä¹‰åœ¨ java.util åŒ…ä¸­
    - ç”¨äºä»å„ç§è¾“å…¥æºï¼ˆå¦‚ System.inã€æ–‡ä»¶ï¼‰è¯»å–æ•°æ®

2. è¾“å…¥æºçš„æŒ‡å®š

    - æ„é€ æ–¹æ³•ä¸­ä¼ å…¥è¾“å…¥æµï¼ˆå¦‚ System.inï¼‰
    - å¯æ ¹æ®éœ€æ±‚è¯»å–é”®ç›˜è¾“å…¥æˆ–æ–‡ä»¶æ•°æ®

3. å¸¸ç”¨è¯»å–æ–¹æ³•

    - `next()`ï¼šè¯»å–ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ª tokenï¼ˆä»¥ç©ºæ ¼åˆ†éš”ï¼‰
    - `nextLine()`ï¼šè¯»å–æ•´è¡Œè¾“å…¥ï¼ŒåŒ…å«ç©ºæ ¼
    - `nextInt()/nextByte()/nextDouble()`ï¼šè¯»å–å¯¹åº”ç±»å‹çš„æ•°å€¼
    - `trim()`ï¼šå»é™¤å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å‰åå¤šä½™ç©ºç™½

**ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹**

1. å¸¸ç”¨è¯»å–æ–¹æ³•

    ```java
    Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

    // è¾“å…¥æ•´æ•°
    System.out.print("è¯·è¾“å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªæ•´æ•°ï¼š");
    int x = scanner.nextInt();
    System.out.println("ä½ è¾“å…¥çš„æ•´æ•°æ˜¯ï¼š" + x);

    // è¾“å…¥å°æ•°
    System.out.print("\nè¯·è¾“å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªå°æ•°ï¼š");
    double y = scanner.nextDouble();
    System.out.println("ä½ è¾“å…¥çš„å°æ•°æ˜¯ï¼š" + y);

    // æ¸…é™¤æ¢è¡Œç¬¦
    scanner.nextLine();  // å¤„ç† nextInt() / nextDouble() åæ®‹ç•™çš„æ¢è¡Œç¬¦

    // è¾“å…¥å•ä¸ªå•è¯ï¼ˆä¸åŒ…æ‹¬ç©ºæ ¼ï¼‰
    System.out.print("\nè¯·è¾“å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªå•è¯ï¼ˆé‡åˆ°ç©ºæ ¼åœæ­¢ï¼‰ï¼š");
    String s = scanner.next();
    System.out.println("ä½ è¾“å…¥çš„å•è¯æ˜¯ï¼š" + s);
    scanner.nextLine();  // å¤„ç† next() åçš„æ¢è¡Œç¬¦

    // è¾“å…¥æ•´è¡Œå­—ç¬¦ä¸²
    System.out.print("\nè¯·è¾“å…¥ä¸€æ•´è¡Œæ–‡æœ¬ï¼š");
    String s2 = scanner.nextLine();
    System.out.println("ä½ è¾“å…¥çš„æ•´è¡Œæ–‡æœ¬æ˜¯ï¼š" + s2);

    // è¾“å…¥æ•´è¡Œæ–‡æœ¬ï¼ˆå»é™¤é¦–å°¾ç©ºæ ¼ï¼‰
    System.out.print("\nè¯·è¾“å…¥ä¸€æ•´è¡Œæ–‡æœ¬ï¼ˆè‡ªåŠ¨å»é™¤å‰åç©ºæ ¼ï¼‰ï¼š");
    String s3 = scanner.nextLine().trim();
    System.out.println("å»é™¤ç©ºæ ¼åçš„æ–‡æœ¬æ˜¯ï¼š" + s3);

    scanner.close(); // å…³é—­ Scanner
    ```

    - è¯´æ˜ï¼š `next()` åªè¯»å–å•ä¸ªå•è¯ï¼Œ`nextLine()` å¯è¯»å–æ•´è¡Œï¼Œç”¨ `trim()` å¯æ¸…é™¤å¤šä½™ç©ºæ ¼ã€‚

## Ex: æŠµæŠ¼è´·æ¬¾è®¡ç®—å™¨

> **è¦æ±‚**ï¼š  
> ç¼–å†™ä¸€ä¸ªç¨‹åºï¼Œè¦æ±‚ç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥è´·æ¬¾æœ¬é‡‘ã€å¹´åˆ©ç‡åŠè´·æ¬¾å¹´é™ï¼Œç„¶åè®¡ç®—å‡ºæ¯æœˆè¿˜æ¬¾é‡‘é¢ï¼Œå¹¶ä»¥è´§å¸æ ¼å¼æ˜¾ç¤ºã€‚è®¡ç®—å‰äº†è§£è´·æ¬¾è®¡ç®—æ–¹å¼ï¼šhttps://www.wikihow.com/Calculate-Mortgage-Payments
>
> **ç¤ºä¾‹**ï¼š
>
> -   è¾“å…¥æœ¬é‡‘ 100000ï¼Œå¹´åˆ©ç‡ 3.92ï¼Œåˆ†æœŸå¹´æ•° 30ï¼Œæœ€åè®¡ç®—å‡ºæ¯æœˆè¿˜æ¬¾é‡‘é¢ä¸º $472.81
>
> **è§£æ³•**ï¼šè·å–è¾“å…¥ï¼Œå¤„ç†å¾—åˆ°çš„å€¼ï¼Œè®¡ç®—ç»“æœï¼Œæ ¼å¼åŒ–ç»“æœè¾“å‡ºï¼Œå…¶ä¸­æŒ‡æ•°è¿ç®—ä½¿ç”¨ Math.pow æ–¹æ³•ã€‚
>
> **æœ€ä½³å®è·µ**
>
> -   ä½¿ç”¨é€‚åˆçš„åŸºæœ¬ç±»å‹ï¼šå°æ•°ç”¨å°å­—èŠ‚æè¿°ï¼Œå¤§æ•°ç”¨å¤§å­—èŠ‚æè¿°
> -   é¿å…é­”æ³•æ•°å­—ï¼šå°†å›ºå®šå€¼ï¼ˆå¦‚ 12ã€100ï¼‰å®šä¹‰ä¸ºå¸¸é‡ï¼ˆå¦‚ MONTHS_IN_YEARã€PERCENTï¼‰ã€‚
> -   æœ‰æ„ä¹‰çš„å˜é‡å‘½åï¼šä½¿ç”¨æè¿°æ€§å˜é‡åï¼Œä½¿ä»£ç ç›´è§‚æ˜“æ‡‚ã€‚
> -   åˆ†æ­¥å¤„ç†å¤æ‚è¡¨è¾¾å¼ï¼šå°†è®¡ç®—è¿‡ç¨‹æ‹†è§£æˆå¤šä¸ªæ­¥éª¤ï¼Œä¾¿äºç»´æŠ¤ä¸è°ƒè¯•ã€‚
> -   ä»£ç å¯è¯»æ€§ï¼šé€‚å½“æ‹†åˆ†é•¿è¡¨è¾¾å¼ï¼Œå¢åŠ ä¸­é—´å˜é‡ï¼Œä½¿ä»£ç é€»è¾‘æ›´æ¸…æ™°ã€‚
>
> **æ‰©å±•å»ºè®®**
>
> -   æ·»åŠ è¾“å…¥éªŒè¯ï¼Œç¡®ä¿ç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥æœ‰æ•ˆæ•°æ®ï¼Œé˜²æ­¢ç¨‹åºå› éæ³•è¾“å…¥å´©æºƒã€‚
> -   åœ¨åç»­ç« èŠ‚ä¸­ä»‹ç»æ¡ä»¶è¯­å¥ï¼Œåˆ©ç”¨æ¡ä»¶åˆ¤æ–­å®Œå–„è¾“å…¥éªŒè¯é€»è¾‘ã€‚

**ä»£ç **

- ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼š

    ```js
    final byte MONTHS_IN_YEAR = 12;
    final byte PERCENTAGE = 100;

    Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

    System.out.print("Principal: ");
    int principal = scanner.nextInt();// æ•°é¢

    System.out.print("Annual Interest Rate:");
    float annualInterestRate = scanner.nextFloat() / PERCENTAGE;// åˆ©ç‡
    float monthlyInterestRate = annualInterestRate / MONTHS_IN_YEAR;
    System.out.print("Period(Years):");
    byte periodYear = scanner.nextByte();// åˆ†æœŸå¹´æ•°
    int periodMonth = periodYear * MONTHS_IN_YEAR;


    double monthlyMortgage = principal
    		* monthlyInterestRate * Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth)
    		/ (Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth) - 1);

    String monthlyMortgageFormatted = NumberFormat.getCurrencyInstance().format(monthlyMortgage);

    System.out.println("Monthly mortgage: " + monthlyMortgageFormatted);
    ```

# Control Flow

## æ¯”è¾ƒè¿ç®—ç¬¦

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šæ¯”è¾ƒè¿ç®—ç¬¦ç”¨äºæ¯”è¾ƒåŸºæœ¬æ•°æ®ç±»å‹çš„å€¼ï¼Œç”Ÿæˆå¸ƒå°”å€¼ï¼ˆ`true` æˆ– `false`ï¼‰ï¼Œä»è€Œåˆ¤æ–­ä¸¤ä¸ªå€¼æ˜¯å¦ç›¸ç­‰æˆ–æ»¡è¶³æŸç§å¤§å°å…³ç³»ï¼Œå¸¸ç”¨äºæ¡ä»¶åˆ¤æ–­å’Œæµç¨‹æ§åˆ¶ã€‚

**çŸ¥è¯†æ ‘**

1. æ¯”è¾ƒè¿ç®—ç¬¦æ¦‚å¿µ

    - åˆ¤æ–­ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°æ®æ˜¯å¦æ»¡è¶³ç‰¹å®šå…³ç³»ï¼ˆç›¸ç­‰ã€ä¸ç­‰ã€å¤§å°æ¯”è¾ƒï¼‰

2. åŸºæœ¬æ¯”è¾ƒè¿ç®—ç¬¦

    - ç­‰äºï¼š`==`ï¼ˆæ³¨æ„ä¸èµ‹å€¼ç¬¦ `=` åŒºåˆ†ï¼‰
    - ä¸ç­‰äºï¼š`!=`

3. å¤§å°æ¯”è¾ƒè¿ç®—ç¬¦

    - å¤§äºï¼š`>`
    - å¤§äºç­‰äºï¼š`>=`
    - å°äºï¼š`<`
    - å°äºç­‰äºï¼š`<=`

4. å¸ƒå°”è¡¨è¾¾å¼ä¸åº”ç”¨

    - æ¯”è¾ƒè¿ç®—è¿”å›å¸ƒå°”å€¼ï¼Œæ„æˆæ¡ä»¶è¡¨è¾¾å¼
    - ç”¨äº ifã€while ç­‰æ§åˆ¶ç»“æ„ï¼Œé©±åŠ¨ç¨‹åºé€»è¾‘

**ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹**

1. åŸºæœ¬ç›¸ç­‰å’Œä¸ç­‰åˆ¤æ–­

    ```java

    int y = 5;
    System.out.println(x == y); // è¾“å‡º trueï¼Œå› ä¸º x ä¸ y ç›¸ç­‰
    System.out.println(x != y); // è¾“å‡º falseï¼Œå› ä¸º x ä¸ y ç›¸ç­‰
    ```

2. å¤§å°æ¯”è¾ƒç¤ºä¾‹

    ```java
    int a = 7;
    int b = 10;
    System.out.println(a > b);  // è¾“å‡º falseï¼Œå› ä¸º 7 ä¸å¤§äº 10
    System.out.println(a >= b); // è¾“å‡º falseï¼Œå› ä¸º 7 æ—¢ä¸å¤§äºä¹Ÿä¸ç­‰äº 10
    System.out.println(a < b);  // è¾“å‡º trueï¼Œå› ä¸º 7 å°äº 10
    System.out.println(a <= b); // è¾“å‡º trueï¼Œå› ä¸º 7 å°äº 10
    ```

## å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ¯”è¾ƒ

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šå­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ¯”è¾ƒç”¨äºåˆ¤æ–­ä¸¤ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²å†…å®¹æ˜¯å¦ä¸€è‡´ï¼Œéœ€åŒºåˆ†ä½¿ç”¨ `==`ï¼ˆæ¯”è¾ƒå¼•ç”¨ï¼‰ä¸ `equals()`ï¼ˆæ¯”è¾ƒå†…å®¹ï¼‰ã€‚å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ± ä¼˜åŒ–å†…å­˜ç®¡ç†ï¼Œ`intern()` æ–¹æ³•å¯å°†å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ‰‹åŠ¨åŠ å…¥æ± ä¸­ï¼Œå®ç°å¯¹è±¡å…±äº«ã€‚

**çŸ¥è¯†æ ‘**

1. `equals()` æ–¹æ³•

    - æ¯”è¾ƒå­—ç¬¦ä¸²å†…å®¹ï¼Œè€Œéå¼•ç”¨åœ°å€

2. å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ± 

    - Java è‡ªåŠ¨ç»´æŠ¤çš„å†…å­˜åŒºåŸŸï¼Œç”¨äºå­˜å‚¨å¸¸é‡å­—ç¬¦ä¸²
    - ç›¸åŒå­—é¢é‡è‡ªåŠ¨å…±äº«å¯¹è±¡ï¼ˆå¼•ç”¨åœ°å€ï¼‰

3. å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ± ä½¿ç”¨åœºæ™¯

    - åº”ç”¨äºç¼“å­˜ã€æ—¥å¿—ã€æ•°æ®åº“æŸ¥è¯¢ç»“æœç­‰ï¼Œé™ä½å†…å­˜å¼€é”€
    - é‡å¤å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å¯è°ƒç”¨ `intern()` å…±äº«å¯¹è±¡
    - æ³¨æ„ï¼šè¿‡åº¦ä½¿ç”¨ intern() å¯èƒ½å¼•èµ·å†…å­˜ä¸è¶³ï¼ˆ**OutOfMemoryError**ï¼‰

4. `==` ä¸ `equals()` åŒºåˆ«

    - `==` æ£€æŸ¥æ˜¯å¦ä¸ºåŒä¸€å¯¹è±¡å¼•ç”¨
    - `equals()` æ£€æŸ¥å¯¹è±¡å†…å®¹æ˜¯å¦ç›¸åŒ

**ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹**

1. å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ¯”è¾ƒ

    ```java
    String a = new String("Str");
    String b = new String("Str");
    System.out.println(a == b);      // false: ä¸åŒå¯¹è±¡å¼•ç”¨
    System.out.println(a.equals(b)); // true: å†…å®¹ç›¸ç­‰
    ```

    - è¯´æ˜ï¼šå±•ç¤ºå¦‚ä½•ä½¿ç”¨ `==` ä¸ `equals()` æ¯”è¾ƒå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ã€‚

2. å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ± 

    ```java
    String a = "hello";
    String b = "hello";
    String c = new String("hello");
    System.out.println(a == b); // true: åŒä¸€å¸¸é‡æ± å¯¹è±¡
    System.out.println(a == c); // false: c ä¸ºæ–°å¯¹è±¡

    String m = "hello" + " world";
    String n = "hello world";
    System.out.println(m == n); // true: ç¼–è¯‘å™¨ä¼˜åŒ–ï¼Œç»“æœä¸ºå¸¸é‡

    String s1 = "hello";
    String s2 = " world";
    String s3 = s1 + s2;
    String s4 = "hello world";
    System.out.println(s3 == s4); // false: åŠ¨æ€æ‹¼æ¥ç”Ÿæˆæ–°å¯¹è±¡

    String x = "hello";
    String y = new String("hello").intern(); // æ‰‹åŠ¨åŠ å…¥å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ± 
    System.out.println(x == y); // true: y ç» intern() åä¸ x ç›¸åŒ
    ```

    - è¯´æ˜ï¼šæ¼”ç¤ºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ± æœºåˆ¶åŠ intern() æ–¹æ³•çš„ä½œç”¨ï¼Œä½¿åŠ¨æ€ç”Ÿæˆçš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å…±äº«å¸¸é‡æ± å¯¹è±¡ã€‚

## é€»è¾‘è¿ç®—ç¬¦

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šé€»è¾‘è¿ç®—ç¬¦ç”¨äºç»„åˆå¤šä¸ªå¸ƒå°”è¡¨è¾¾å¼ï¼Œç”Ÿæˆä¸€ä¸ªæ•´ä½“çš„å¸ƒå°”ç»“æœã€‚å®ƒä»¬åŒ…æ‹¬ä¸ã€æˆ–ã€éï¼Œå¹¶æ”¯æŒçŸ­è·¯æ±‚å€¼ï¼Œå¸¸ç”¨äºæ¡ä»¶åˆ¤æ–­å’Œæµç¨‹æ§åˆ¶ã€‚

**çŸ¥è¯†æ ‘**

1. é€»è¾‘è¿ç®—ç¬¦æ¦‚å¿µ

    - ç”¨äºç»„åˆæˆ–åè½¬å¸ƒå°”è¡¨è¾¾å¼ï¼Œè¾“å‡º true æˆ– false

2. åŸºæœ¬é€»è¾‘è¿ç®—ç¬¦

    - ä¸ï¼ˆANDï¼‰ï¼š`&&`ï¼ˆæˆ– `&`ï¼‰ï¼Œæ‰€æœ‰æ¡ä»¶ä¸º true æ—¶è¿”å› trueâ€˜
    - æˆ–ï¼ˆORï¼‰ï¼š`||`ï¼ˆæˆ– `|`ï¼‰ï¼Œè‡³å°‘ä¸€ä¸ªæ¡ä»¶ä¸º true æ—¶è¿”å› true
    - éï¼ˆNOTï¼‰ï¼š`!`ï¼Œåè½¬å¸ƒå°”å€¼

3. è¿ç®—é¡ºåºä¸çŸ­è·¯æ±‚å€¼

    - çŸ­è·¯æ±‚å€¼ï¼š
        - `&&`ï¼šå½“ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªè¡¨è¾¾å¼ä¸º false æ—¶ï¼Œä¸å†è®¡ç®—åç»­æ¡ä»¶ï¼Œ `&`è®¡ç®—æ‰€æœ‰æ¡ä»¶
        - `||`ï¼šå½“ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªè¡¨è¾¾å¼ä¸º true æ—¶ï¼Œä¸å†è®¡ç®—åç»­æ¡ä»¶ï¼Œ`|`è®¡ç®—æ‰€æœ‰æ¡ä»¶
    - ä½¿ç”¨æ‹¬å·æ˜ç¡®è¿ç®—é¡ºåºï¼Œé¿å…é€»è¾‘æ··æ·†

4. å®é™…åº”ç”¨
    - ç”¨äºå®ç°å¤æ‚é€»è¾‘åˆ¤æ–­ï¼Œå¦‚æƒé™éªŒè¯ã€è´·æ¬¾èµ„æ ¼è¯„ä¼°ç­‰
    - é€šè¿‡åˆç†å‘½åå’Œç»„åˆè¡¨è¾¾å¼ï¼Œæé«˜ä»£ç å¯è¯»æ€§å’Œç»´æŠ¤æ€§

**ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹**

1. ä¸è¿ç®—ç¬¦ç¤ºä¾‹

    ```java
    int temperature = 22;
    // åˆ¤æ–­æ¸©åº¦æ˜¯å¦å¤„äº 20 åˆ° 30 ä¹‹é—´
    boolean isWarm = (temperature > 20) && (temperature < 30);
    System.out.println(isWarm);  // è¾“å‡º true
    ```

2. æˆ–ä¸éè¿ç®—ç¬¦ç»„åˆç¤ºä¾‹

    ```java
    boolean hasHighIncome = true;
    boolean hasGoodCredit = false;
    // æ»¡è¶³ä»»ä¸€æ¡ä»¶åˆ™å¯è´·æ¬¾
    boolean isEligible = hasHighIncome || hasGoodCredit;

    boolean hasCriminalRecord = false;
    // ä»…å½“æ— çŠ¯ç½ªè®°å½•æ—¶ï¼Œèµ„æ ¼æœ‰æ•ˆ
    isEligible = isEligible && (!hasCriminalRecord);
    System.out.println(isEligible);  // è¾“å‡º true
    ```

## if è¯­å¥

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šif è¯­å¥æ ¹æ®æ¡ä»¶åˆ¤æ–­æ§åˆ¶ç¨‹åºæµç¨‹ï¼Œæ”¯æŒå¤šåˆ†æ”¯ï¼ˆ`if`ã€`else if`ã€`else`ï¼‰æ¥æ‰§è¡Œä¸åŒä»£ç å—ï¼Œä¾¿äºå¤„ç†å¤šç§æƒ…å½¢ã€‚

**çŸ¥è¯†æ ‘**

1. `if` è¯­å¥æ¦‚å¿µ

    - æ ¹æ®å¸ƒå°”è¡¨è¾¾å¼çš„çœŸå‡æ‰§è¡Œç›¸åº”ä»£ç 

2. åˆ†æ”¯ç»“æ„


    - è¯´æ˜ï¼šå¾ªç¯ä» i=0 å¼€å§‹ï¼Œæ¯æ¬¡è¿­ä»£åé€’å¢ï¼Œç›´åˆ° i ä¸å°äº 5 æ—¶ç»“æŸã€‚

    ```java
    // å¾ªç¯æ¡ä»¶ï¼šç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥ä¸ç­‰äº "quit"ï¼ˆå¿½ç•¥å¤§å°å†™ï¼‰

    ```

    - è¯´æ˜ï¼šè¯¥ç¤ºä¾‹ä¸æ–­è¯»å–ç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨ toLowerCase() æ ‡å‡†åŒ–è¾“å…¥ï¼Œå†ç”¨ equals æ¯”è¾ƒç»ˆæ­¢æ¡ä»¶ï¼Œå®ç°ç”¨æˆ·åœ¨è¾“å…¥ "quit" åé€€å‡ºå¾ªç¯ã€‚

## do while å¾ªç¯

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šdo while å¾ªç¯å…ˆæ‰§è¡Œå¾ªç¯ä½“ï¼Œå†åˆ¤æ–­æ¡ä»¶ï¼Œä¿è¯å¾ªç¯ä½“è‡³å°‘æ‰§è¡Œä¸€æ¬¡ï¼Œé€‚ç”¨äºéœ€è¦åœ¨æ¡ä»¶æ£€æŸ¥å‰å¿…æ‰§è¡Œæ“ä½œçš„åœºæ™¯ã€‚

## for-each å¾ªç¯

## Ex: è´·æ¬¾è®¡ç®—-å¸¦è¾“å…¥éªŒè¯

> **è¦æ±‚**ï¼šæ‰©å±•æŠµæŠ¼è´·æ¬¾è®¡ç®—å™¨ï¼Œè¦æ±‚ç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥è´·æ¬¾æœ¬é‡‘ã€å¹´åˆ©ç‡åŠè´·æ¬¾å¹´é™ã€‚å¯¹æ¯ä¸ªè¾“å…¥æ·»åŠ åŸºæœ¬çš„é”™è¯¯å¤„ç†å’ŒéªŒè¯ï¼Œè‹¥è¾“å…¥ä¸åˆæ³•åˆ™æŒç»­æç¤ºï¼Œç›´åˆ°ç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥æœ‰æ•ˆæ•°æ®ä¸ºæ­¢ã€‚
>
> **è§£æ³•**ï¼š
>
> 1.  **è¾“å…¥å¤„ç†ä¸éªŒè¯**
>
>     -   åœ¨å¾ªç¯å¤–å£°æ˜ principalã€annualInterest å’Œ years å˜é‡ï¼Œä¿è¯å…¶ä½œç”¨åŸŸåœ¨æ•´ä¸ªæ–¹æ³•ä¸­æœ‰æ•ˆã€‚
>     -   å¯¹æ¯ä¸ªè¾“å…¥ä½¿ç”¨æ— é™å¾ªç¯ï¼ˆwhile trueï¼‰è¿›è¡ŒéªŒè¯ï¼š
>         -   è´·æ¬¾æœ¬é‡‘éœ€å¤§äºæˆ–ç­‰äºè®¾å®šçš„æœ€å°å€¼ï¼ˆä¾‹å¦‚ 1000ï¼‰ï¼›
>         -   å¹´åˆ©ç‡å¿…é¡»å¤§äº 0ï¼›
>         -   è´·æ¬¾å¹´é™å¿…é¡»å¤§äº 0ã€‚
>     -   è‹¥è¾“å…¥æ— æ•ˆï¼Œåˆ™æ‰“å°é”™è¯¯æç¤ºå¹¶é‡å¤è¾“å…¥ï¼Œç›´åˆ°è¾“å…¥åˆæ³•ã€‚
>
> 2.  **è®¡ç®—å¤„ç†**
>
>     -   å…¶ä¸­æŒ‡æ•°è¿ç®—ä½¿ç”¨ Math.pow æ–¹æ³•ã€‚

**ä»£ç **

- ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹

    ```java
    final byte MONTHS_IN_YEAR = 12;
    final byte PERCENTAGE = 100;

    int principal = 0;
    float monthlyInterestRate = 0;
    int periodMonth = 0;

    Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

    while (true) {
    	System.out.print("Principal: ");
    	principal = scanner.nextInt();// æ•°é¢
    	if (principal >= 1000 || principal <= 1_000_000) {
    		break;
    	}
    	System.out.print("Enter a value between 1000 and 1_000_000");
    }
    while (true) {
    	System.out.print("Annual Interest Rate:");
    	float annualInterestRate = scanner.nextFloat() / PERCENTAGE;// åˆ©ç‡
    	if (annualInterestRate >= 0 && annualInterestRate <= 30) {
    		monthlyInterestRate = annualInterestRate / MONTHS_IN_YEAR;
    		break;
    	}
    	System.out.print("Enter a value between 1 and 30");

    }

    while (true) {
    	System.out.print("Period(Years):");
    	byte periodYear = scanner.nextByte();// åˆ†æœŸå¹´æ•°
    	if (periodYear >= 0 && periodYear <= 30) {
    		periodMonth = periodYear * MONTHS_IN_YEAR;
    		break;
    	}
    	System.out.print("Enter a value between 1 and 30");
    }

    double monthlyMortgage = principal
    		* monthlyInterestRate * Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth)
    		/ (Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth) - 1);

    String monthlyMortgageFormatted = NumberFormat.getCurrencyInstance().format(monthlyMortgage);

    System.out.println("Monthly mortgage: " + monthlyMortgageFormatted);
    ```

# Clean Coding

## Clean Code

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šé€šè¿‡æ•´æ´ç¼–ç ï¼Œå°†ç¨‹åºæ‹†åˆ†æˆç‹¬ç«‹å°å—ï¼Œåˆ©ç”¨æ–¹æ³•æå–å®ç°æ¨¡å—åŒ–ã€‚è¿™æ ·ä»£ç å°±åƒæ•´æ´çš„æˆ¿é—´ï¼Œæ¯ä¸ªç‰©å“éƒ½æœ‰å½’å¤„ï¼Œæé«˜äº†å¯è¯»æ€§ã€å¯ç»´æŠ¤æ€§å’Œé‡ç”¨æ€§ã€‚

**çŸ¥è¯†æ ‘**

1. ä»£ç æ•´æ´æ¦‚å¿µ

    - æ¯ä¸ªäººéƒ½å¯ä»¥å†™è®¡ç®—æœºèƒ½ç†è§£çš„ä»£ç ï¼Œä¼˜ç§€çš„ç¨‹åºå‘˜ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å†™å‡ºæ™®é€šäººå°±èƒ½ç†è§£çš„ä»£ç 
    - ç±»æ¯”æ•´ç†æˆ¿é—´ï¼šäº•ç„¶æœ‰åºçš„ä»£ç ä¾¿äºæŸ¥æ‰¾ä¸ç»´æŠ¤

2. æ¨¡å—åŒ–ä¸æ–¹æ³•æå–

    - å°†é‡å¤æˆ–å¤æ‚ä»£ç å°è£…ä¸ºç‹¬ç«‹æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œå‡å°‘å†—ä½™
    - æ–¹æ³•åç§°åº”è¯­ä¹‰æ˜ç¡®ï¼Œä¾¿äºç†è§£

3. æ•´æ´ç¼–ç çš„å¥½å¤„

    - æé«˜ä»£ç å¯è¯»æ€§ä¸æ‰©å±•æ€§
    - é™ä½é”™è¯¯ç‡ï¼Œä¾¿äºå›¢é˜Ÿåä½œä¸è°ƒè¯•

## åˆ›å»ºä¸è°ƒç”¨æ–¹æ³•

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šæ–¹æ³•å°†ä»£ç æ‹†åˆ†æˆç‹¬ç«‹æ¨¡å—ï¼Œä½¿å¤æ‚é€»è¾‘æ˜“äºç»´æŠ¤å’Œé‡ç”¨ã€‚é€šè¿‡å®šä¹‰æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œå¯å°†é‡å¤æˆ–å¤æ‚æ“ä½œå°è£…ï¼Œæå‡ä»£ç æ¸…æ™°åº¦å’Œå¯è¯»æ€§ã€‚

**çŸ¥è¯†æ ‘**

1. æ–¹æ³•çš„åŸºæœ¬æ¦‚å¿µ

    - ç‹¬ç«‹ä»£ç å—ï¼šå°è£…ç‰¹å®šä»»åŠ¡
    - å®šä¹‰åœ¨ç±»ä¸­ï¼Œä¸ç±»æˆ–å¯¹è±¡å…³è”

2. æ–¹æ³•çš„å®šä¹‰

    - è®¿é—®ä¿®é¥°ç¬¦ï¼špublicã€private ç­‰å†³å®šå¯è§æ€§ï¼Œpulic æ„å‘³ç€æ–¹æ³•å¯ä»¥ä» lclass å¤–éƒ¨è®¿é—®ï¼Œå…·ä½“ç”¨æ³•åç»­è®²è§£ã€‚
    - static å…³é”®å­—ï¼šå£°æ˜æ–¹æ³•å±äºç±»ï¼Œå…·ä½“ç”¨æ³•åç»­è®²è§£ã€‚
    - è¿”å›ç±»å‹ï¼švoid æˆ–å…·ä½“æ•°æ®ç±»å‹ï¼Œå£°æ˜æ–¹æ³•è¿”å›çš„æ•°æ®
    - æ–¹æ³•åï¼šä½¿ç”¨ camelCase å‘½åï¼Œæè¿°å…¶åŠŸèƒ½

3. å‚æ•°ä¸è¿”å›

    - å‚æ•°åˆ—è¡¨ï¼šæ”¾åœ¨åœ†æ‹¬å·ä¸­ï¼Œç”¨é€—å·åˆ†éš”ï¼Œä½œä¸ºè¾“å…¥
    - æ–¹æ³•ä½“ï¼šç”¨èŠ±æ‹¬å·åŒ…è£¹ï¼ŒåŒ…å«å±€éƒ¨å˜é‡å’Œé€»è¾‘
    - return è¯­å¥ï¼šè¿”å›å€¼ï¼ˆå¿…é¡»ä¸è¿”å›ç±»å‹ä¸€è‡´ï¼‰ï¼Œè‹¥æ— è¿”å›åˆ™ä½¿ç”¨ void

4. æ–¹æ³•è°ƒç”¨ä¸é‡ç”¨
    - åœ¨ main æ–¹æ³•ä¸­è°ƒç”¨ï¼Œä¼ é€’æ‰€éœ€å‚æ•°
    - é‡ç”¨æ–¹æ³•é¿å…ä»£ç å†—ä½™ï¼Œå®ç°æ¨¡å—åŒ–

**ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹**

1. ç®€å•é—®å€™æ–¹æ³•ï¼ˆæ— è¿”å›å€¼ï¼‰

    ```java
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        greetUser("Nancy");
    }

    public static void greetUser(String name) {
        System.out.println("Hello " + name + "!");
    }
    ```

    - è¯´æ˜ï¼šå®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªé™æ€æ–¹æ³• greetUserï¼Œæ¥å—ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²å‚æ•°ï¼Œå¹¶æ‰“å°é—®å€™ä¿¡æ¯ã€‚

2. å¸¦å‚æ•°ä¸è¿”å›å€¼çš„æ–¹æ³•

    ```java
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String message = greetUser("Yi", "Miao");
        System.out.println(message);
    }

    public static String greetUser(String firstName, String lastName) {
        return "Hello " + firstName + " " + lastName + "!";
    }
    ```

    - è¯´æ˜ï¼šå±•ç¤ºå¦‚ä½•å®šä¹‰å’Œè°ƒç”¨ä¸€ä¸ªå¸¦ä¸¤ä¸ªå‚æ•°ä¸”è¿”å›å­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„é—®å€™æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œå®ç°å‚æ•°ä¼ é€’å’Œè¿”å›å€¼å¤„ç†ã€‚

## æå–æ–¹æ³• 1ï¼ˆè´·æ¬¾è®¡ç®—ï¼‰

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šæå–ä¸Šä¸€èŠ‚ç»ƒä¹ ä¸­çš„è®¡ç®—æ–¹æ³•

**ä»£ç **

- ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹

    ```java
    package com.pang;

    import java.text.NumberFormat;
    import java.util.Scanner;

    public class Main {
        public static void main(String[] args) {

            int principal = 0;
            float annualInterestRate = 0;
            byte periodYear = 0;

            Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

            while (true) {
                System.out.print("Principal: ");
                principal = scanner.nextInt();// æ•°é¢
                if (principal >= 1000 || principal <= 1_000_000) {
                    break;
                }
                System.out.print("Enter a value between 1000 and 1_000_000");
            }
            while (true) {
                System.out.print("Annual Interest Rate:");
                annualInterestRate = scanner.nextFloat();// åˆ©ç‡
                if (annualInterestRate >= 0 && annualInterestRate <= 30)
                    break;
                System.out.print("Enter a value between 1 and 30");

            }

            while (true) {
                System.out.print("Period(Years):");
                periodYear = scanner.nextByte();// åˆ†æœŸå¹´æ•°
                if (periodYear >= 0 && periodYear <= 30)
                    break;
                System.out.print("Enter a value between 1 and 30");
            }

            double monthlyMortgage = caculateMortgage(principal, annualInterestRate, periodYear);

            String monthlyMortgageFormatted = NumberFormat.getCurrencyInstance().format(monthlyMortgage);
            System.out.println("Monthly mortgage: " + monthlyMortgageFormatted);
        }

        public static double caculateMortgage(
                int principal,
                float annualInterestRate,
                byte periodYear) {

            final byte MONTHS_IN_YEAR = 12;
            final byte PERCENTAGE = 100;

            float monthlyInterestRate = annualInterestRate / MONTHS_IN_YEAR / PERCENTAGE;
            int periodMonth = periodYear * MONTHS_IN_YEAR;

            double monthlyMortgage = principal
                    - monthlyInterestRate * Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth)
                    / (Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth) - 1);

            return monthlyMortgage;
        }
    }
    ```

## æå–æ–¹æ³• 2ï¼ˆè´·æ¬¾è®¡ç®—ï¼‰

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šæå–ä¸Šä¸€èŠ‚ç»ƒä¹ ä¸­çš„è¯»å–æ–¹æ³•

**ä»£ç **

- ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹

    ```java
    public static void main(String[] args) {

    	int principal = 0;
    	float annualInterestRate = 0;
    	byte periodYear = 0;

    	Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

    	principal = (int) readNumber("Principal: ", 1000, 1_000_000);
    	annualInterestRate = (float) readNumber("Annual Interest Rate: ", 1, 30);
    	periodYear = (byte) readNumber("Period Year: ", 1, 30);

    	double monthlyMortgage = caculateMortgage(principal, annualInterestRate, periodYear);

    	String monthlyMortgageFormatted = NumberFormat.getCurrencyInstance().format(monthlyMortgage);
    	System.out.println("Monthly mortgage: " + monthlyMortgageFormatted);
    }

    public static double readNumber(String prompt, double min, double max) {
    	Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);
    	double value;
    	while (true) {
    		System.out.print(prompt);
    		value = scanner.nextFloat();
    		if (value >= min && value <= max) break;
    		System.out.print("Enter a value between " + min + " and " + max);
    	}
    	return value;
    }

    public static double caculateMortgage(
    		int principal,
    		float annualInterestRate,
    		byte periodYear) {

    	final byte MONTHS_IN_YEAR = 12;
    	final byte PERCENTAGE = 100;

    	float monthlyInterestRate = annualInterestRate / MONTHS_IN_YEAR / PERCENTAGE;
    	int periodMonth = periodYear * MONTHS_IN_YEAR;

    	double monthlyMortgage = principal
    			* monthlyInterestRate * Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth)
    			/ (Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth) - 1);

    	return monthlyMortgage;
    }
    ```

## Ex: è´·æ¬¾è®¡ç®—-å«è¿˜æ¬¾è®¡åˆ’

> **è¦æ±‚**ï¼šæ‰©å±•æŠµæŠ¼è´·æ¬¾è®¡ç®—å™¨ï¼Œå®ç°å¦‚ä¸‹åŠŸèƒ½ï¼š
>
> -   ç”¨æˆ·è¾“å…¥è´·æ¬¾æœ¬é‡‘ã€å¹´åˆ©ç‡å’Œè´·æ¬¾å¹´é™ï¼›
> -   è®¡ç®—å¹¶è¾“å‡ºæœˆè¿˜æ¬¾é¢ï¼›
> -   è¾“å‡ºæ¯ä¸ªæœˆè¿˜æ¬¾åå‰©ä½™æœ¬é‡‘ï¼ˆè¿˜æ¬¾è®¡åˆ’ï¼‰ã€‚
> -   è®¡ç®—å…¬å¼ï¼šbalance = principal \* ((1 + r)^n - (1 + r)^p) / ((1 + r)^n - 1)
>
> **ç¤ºä¾‹**ï¼š
>
> -   è¾“å…¥æœ¬é‡‘ 180000ï¼Œå¹´åˆ©ç‡ 4ï¼Œåˆ†æœŸå¹´æ•° 10ï¼Œæœ€åè®¡ç®—å‡ºæ¯æœˆè¿˜æ¬¾é‡‘é¢ä¸º $1,822.41ï¼Œæœ€åä¸€æœŸè¿˜æ¬¾é‡‘é¢ä¸º$1,816.36
>
> **è§£æ³•**ï¼š
>
> 1. **é‡æ„è®¡ç®—é€»è¾‘**
>
>     - æå–æœˆè¿˜æ¬¾é¢è®¡ç®—åˆ° `calculateMortgage` æ–¹æ³•ï¼›
>     - æå–å‰©ä½™æœ¬é‡‘è®¡ç®—åˆ° `calculateBalance` æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œå…¬å¼ä¸º
>         ```
>         balance = principal * ((1 + r)^n - (1 + r)^p) / ((1 + r)^n - 1)
>         ```
>         å…¶ä¸­ r ä¸ºæœˆåˆ©ç‡ï¼Œn ä¸ºæ€»è¿˜æ¬¾æœŸæ•°ï¼Œp ä¸ºå·²ä»˜æ¬¾æ¬¡æ•°ã€‚
>
> 2. **ä¼˜åŒ–ä»£ç ç»“æ„**
>     - å°†å¸¸é‡ï¼ˆå¦‚ MONTHS_IN_YEARã€PERCENTï¼‰å®šä¹‰ä¸ºç±»çº§åˆ«çš„é™æ€å­—æ®µï¼›
>     - æŠ½å–é€šç”¨è¾“å…¥éªŒè¯æ–¹æ³• `readNumber`ï¼Œç»Ÿä¸€è·å–åˆæ³•è¾“å…¥ï¼›
>     - åœ¨ main æ–¹æ³•ä¸­è°ƒç”¨å„æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œä¾æ¬¡è¾“å‡ºæœˆè¿˜æ¬¾é¢åŠæ”¯ä»˜è®¡åˆ’ã€‚

**ä»£ç **

- ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹

```java
package com.pang;

import java.text.NumberFormat;
import java.util.Scanner;

public class Main {
    final static byte MONTHS_IN_YEAR = 12;
    final static byte PERCENTAGE = 100;

    public static void main(String[] args) {

        int principal = 0;
        float annualInterestRate = 0;
        byte periodYear = 0;

        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

        principal = (int) readNumber("Principal: ", 1000, 1_000_000);
        annualInterestRate = (float) readNumber("Annual Interest Rate: ", 1, 30);
        periodYear = (byte) readNumber("Period Year: ", 1, 30);

        double monthlyMortgage = caculateMortgage(principal, annualInterestRate, periodYear);

        String monthlyMortgageFormatted = NumberFormat.getCurrencyInstance().format(monthlyMortgage);
        System.out.println("\nMortgage");
        System.out.println("---------");
        System.out.println("Monthly Payment: " + monthlyMortgageFormatted);
        System.out.println("\nPayment Schedule");
        System.out.println("----------------");
        for (short month = 1; month <= periodYear * MONTHS_IN_YEAR; month++) {
            double balance = caculateBalance(principal, annualInterestRate, periodYear, month);
            System.out.println(NumberFormat.getCurrencyInstance().format(balance));

        }
    }

    public static double readNumber(String prompt, double min, double max) {
        Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);
        double value;
        while (true) {
            System.out.print(prompt);
            value = scanner.nextFloat();
            if (value >= min && value <= max) break;
            System.out.print("Enter a value between " + min + " and " + max);
        }
        return value;
    }

    public static double caculateMortgage(
            int principal,
            float annualInterestRate,
            byte periodYear) {

        float monthlyInterestRate = annualInterestRate / MONTHS_IN_YEAR / PERCENTAGE;
        int periodMonth = periodYear * MONTHS_IN_YEAR;

        double monthlyMortgage = principal
                - monthlyInterestRate * Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth)
                / (Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth) - 1);

        return monthlyMortgage;
    }

    public static double caculateBalance(
            int principal,
            float annualInterestRate,
            byte periodYear,
            short paymentsMade) {

        float monthlyInterestRate = annualInterestRate / MONTHS_IN_YEAR / PERCENTAGE;
        int periodMonth = periodYear * MONTHS_IN_YEAR;

        double banlance = principal *
                (Math.pow((1 + monthlyInterestRate), periodMonth)
                        - Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, paymentsMade))
                / (Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth) - 1);

        return banlance;
    }
}
```

## Ex: è´·æ¬¾è®¡ç®—-æ–¹æ³•æå–

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šä½¿ç”¨ IDEA è‡ªå¸¦çš„æ–¹æ³•æå–å·¥å…·ï¼Œè¿›ä¸€æ­¥ä¼˜åŒ–ä»£ç ç»“æ„
> æ–¹å¼ï¼šCommond+option+M æå–æ–¹æ³•ï¼šé€‰å–ä»£ç â€”â€”ç½®é¡¶èœå• Refactorâ€”â€”Extract/Introduceâ€”â€”Method
> æ³¨æ„ï¼šä½¿ç”¨ Extract å·¥å…·ç”Ÿæˆçš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œé»˜è®¤ä¸º private

**ä»£ç **

- ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹

    ```java
    package com.pang;

    import java.text.NumberFormat;
    import java.util.Scanner;

    public class Main {
      final static byte MONTHS_IN_YEAR = 12;
      final static byte PERCENTAGE = 100;

      public static void main(String[] args) {
          Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

          int principal = (int) readNumber("Principal: ", 1000, 1_000_000);
          float annualInterestRate = (float) readNumber("Annual Interest Rate: ", 1, 30);
          byte periodYear = (byte) readNumber("Period Year: ", 1, 30);

          printMortgage(principal, annualInterestRate, periodYear);
          printPaymentsSchedule(periodYear, principal, annualInterestRate);
      }

      private static void printMortgage(int principal, float annualInterestRate, byte periodYear) {
          double monthlyMortgage = caculateMortgage(principal, annualInterestRate, periodYear);

          String monthlyMortgageFormatted = NumberFormat.getCurrencyInstance().format(monthlyMortgage);
          System.out.println("\nMortgage");
          System.out.println("---------");
          System.out.println("Monthly Payment: " + monthlyMortgageFormatted);
      }

      private static void printPaymentsSchedule(byte periodYear, int principal, float annualInterestRate) {
          System.out.println("\nPayment Schedule");
          System.out.println("----------------");
          for (short month = 1; month <= periodYear * MONTHS_IN_YEAR; month++) {
              double balance = caculateBalance(principal, annualInterestRate, periodYear, month);
              System.out.println(NumberFormat.getCurrencyInstance().format(balance));

          }
      }

      public static double readNumber(String prompt, double min, double max) {
          Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);
          double value;
          while (true) {
              System.out.print(prompt);
              value = scanner.nextFloat();
              if (value >= min && value <= max) break;
              System.out.print("Enter a value between " + min + " and " + max);
          }
          return value;
      }

      public static double caculateMortgage(
              int principal,
              float annualInterestRate,
              byte periodYear) {

          float monthlyInterestRate = annualInterestRate / MONTHS_IN_YEAR / PERCENTAGE;
          int periodMonth = periodYear * MONTHS_IN_YEAR;

          double monthlyMortgage = principal
                  - monthlyInterestRate * Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth)
                  / (Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth) - 1);

          return monthlyMortgage;
      }

      public static double caculateBalance(
              int principal,
              float annualInterestRate,
              byte periodYear,
              short paymentsMade) {

          float monthlyInterestRate = annualInterestRate / MONTHS_IN_YEAR / PERCENTAGE;
          int periodMonth = periodYear * MONTHS_IN_YEAR;

          double banlance = principal *
                  (Math.pow((1 + monthlyInterestRate), periodMonth)
                          - Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, paymentsMade))
                  / (Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth) - 1);

          return banlance;
      }
    }
    ```

## è°ƒè¯• Debug

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šè°ƒè¯•æ˜¯å‘ç°å’Œä¿®å¤ç¨‹åºé”™è¯¯çš„è¿‡ç¨‹ã€‚åˆ©ç”¨æ–­ç‚¹ã€å•æ­¥æ‰§è¡Œã€å˜é‡ç›‘æ§ã€è°ƒç”¨å †æ ˆå’Œç›‘è§†è¡¨è¾¾å¼ç­‰å·¥å…·ï¼Œå¯ä»¥é€è¡Œæ£€æŸ¥ä»£ç ï¼Œå®šä½é—®é¢˜å¹¶éªŒè¯ä¿®å¤ï¼Œä»è€Œæé«˜ä»£ç è´¨é‡å’Œå¼€å‘æ•ˆç‡ã€‚

## æ‰“åŒ… Package

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šéƒ¨ç½² Java åº”ç”¨ç¨‹åºæ˜¯å°†ç¼–è¯‘åçš„ä»£ç åŠèµ„æºæ‰“åŒ…æˆ jar æ–‡ä»¶ï¼Œä¾›ç”¨æˆ·åœ¨å®‰è£…äº† Java è¿è¡Œç¯å¢ƒçš„ç³»ç»Ÿä¸Šç‹¬ç«‹è¿è¡Œã€‚è¿™ä¸€è¿‡ç¨‹ç¡®ä¿ä»£ç åˆ†å‘ã€è·¨å¹³å°æ‰§è¡Œå’Œç»´æŠ¤çš„ä¾¿æ·æ€§ã€‚

**çŸ¥è¯†æ ‘**

1. Jar æ–‡ä»¶æ¦‚å¿µ

    - Java Archive æ ¼å¼ï¼ŒåŒ…å« .class æ–‡ä»¶å’Œèµ„æº
    - ä¾¿äºåˆ†å‘å’Œè·¨å¹³å°æ‰§è¡Œ

2. æ„å»ºä¸æ‰“åŒ…

    - åœ¨ IntelliJ ä¸­é…ç½® Artifactï¼ˆFileâ€”â€”Project Structureâ€”â€”Artifactï¼‰
    - é€‰æ‹©é¡¹ç›®æ¨¡å— Jarï¼ˆJarFx æ˜¯æ¡Œé¢åº”ç”¨ï¼‰ã€ä¸»ç±»åŠä¾èµ–é¡¹ï¼ˆé€‰æ‹© From modules with dependencies...ï¼Œéšåé€‰æ‹© Main class ï¼‰ï¼Œç”Ÿæˆ jar æ–‡ä»¶
    - ä½¿ç”¨ â€œBuild Artifactâ€ å®Œæˆæ‰“åŒ…ï¼ˆBuild â€”â€”Build Artifactâ€”â€”Buildï¼‰
    - åœ¨ç”Ÿæˆçš„ out ç›®å½•æœ€åçš„å±‚çº§ä¸‹ï¼Œå¯ä»¥çœ‹åˆ°ç”Ÿæˆçš„ jar æ–‡ä»¶

3. éƒ¨ç½²ä¸æ‰§è¡Œ

    - ç›®æ ‡æœºå™¨å¿…é¡»å®‰è£… Java è¿è¡Œç¯å¢ƒ
    - é€šè¿‡å‘½ä»¤è¡Œæ‰§è¡Œï¼Œåœ¨è¯¥æ–‡ä»¶æ‰€åœ¨è·¯å¾„æ‰“å¼€ç»ˆç«¯ï¼Œè¾“å…¥ï¼š`java -jar HelloWorld.jar`
    - æ³¨æ„æ–‡ä»¶è·¯å¾„åŠå¤§å°å†™æ•æ„Ÿæ€§ï¼ˆç‰¹åˆ«åœ¨ Linux/Macï¼‰

**ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹**

1. ä»£ç æ–‡ä»¶ç¤ºä¾‹

    ```java
    package com.pang;

    public class Main {
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println("Hello World");// åœ¨æ­¤å¤„è®¾ç½®æ–­ç‚¹
        }
    }
    ```

2. è¿è¡Œ jar æ–‡ä»¶ç¤ºä¾‹


> ç®€è¿°ï¼šåˆ©ç”¨ getter å’Œ setter æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œå¯ä»¥åœ¨è®¾ç½®æ•°æ®æ—¶è¿›è¡ŒéªŒè¯ï¼Œæå‡ç³»ç»Ÿå¥å£®æ€§ã€‚

    - Getterï¼šè·å–ç§æœ‰å­—æ®µçš„å€¼ã€‚
    - Setterï¼šä¿®æ”¹ç§æœ‰å­—æ®µçš„å€¼å¹¶å¯ä»¥è¿›è¡Œåˆæ³•æ€§æ ¡éªŒã€‚

2. æ•°æ®éªŒè¯ä¸è®¿é—®æ§åˆ¶

    - å­—æ®µç§æœ‰åŒ–ï¼ˆprivateï¼‰ï¼šç¦æ­¢å¤–éƒ¨ç›´æ¥è®¿é—®ï¼Œä¿è¯æ•°æ®å®‰å…¨ã€‚
    - ç»Ÿä¸€éªŒè¯é€»è¾‘ï¼šé¿å…æ¯æ¬¡è®¿é—®é‡å¤éªŒè¯ï¼Œé™ä½ç»´æŠ¤æˆæœ¬ã€‚

3. è‡ªåŠ¨ç”Ÿæˆ Getter/Setter æŠ€å·§

    - å¿«æ·é”®ï¼ˆå¦‚ IDEAï¼šCmd+N æˆ– Alt+Insertï¼‰ï¼šå¿«é€Ÿç”Ÿæˆ getter/setter æ–¹æ³•ã€‚
    - Refactor èœå•ï¼šå³é”®å­—æ®µï¼Œé€‰æ‹© Refactor -> Encapsulate Fieldsã€‚
    - é»˜è®¤ç”Ÿæˆå¸¦ public ä¿®é¥°ç¬¦çš„ setter/getter

**ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹**

1. è‡ªå®šä¹‰ setter æ–¹æ³•å®ç°æ•°æ®éªŒè¯

    ```java
    public class Employee {
        private int baseSalary;
        private int hourlyRate;

        public int calculateSalary(int extraHours) {
            return getBaseSalary() + (getHourlyRate() * extraHours);
        }

        public void setBaseSalary(int baseSalary) {
            if (baseSalary <= 0)
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("Base Salary cannot be 0 or less.");
            this.baseSalary = baseSalary;
        }

        public int getBaseSalary() {
            return baseSalary;
        }

        public int getHourlyRate() {
            return hourlyRate;
        }

        public void setHourlyRate(int hourlyRate) {
            if (hourlyRate < 0)
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("Hourly Rate cannot be negative.");
            this.hourlyRate = hourlyRate;
        }
    }
    ```

    - æè¿°ï¼šé€šè¿‡å°† `baseSalary` ã€`baseSalary`è®¾ä¸ºç§æœ‰ï¼Œå¹¶åœ¨ setter ä¸­è¿›è¡ŒéªŒè¯ï¼Œé˜²æ­¢æ— æ•ˆæ•°æ®ï¼›åŒæ—¶æä¾› getter æ–¹æ³•è¯»å–è¯¥å­—æ®µï¼Œé¿å…ç›´æ¥è®¿é—®ã€‚

2. åœ¨ Main ç±»ä¸­ä½¿ç”¨å°è£…åçš„ Employee å¯¹è±¡

    ```java

        var employee = new Employee();
        employee.setBaseSalary(30_000);
        employee.setHourlyRate(20);
        int totalWage = employee.calculateSalary(10);
        System.out.println(totalWage);
    }
    ```

    - æè¿°ï¼š
        - å¤–éƒ¨è°ƒç”¨ setter è®¾ç½®å€¼ï¼Œé€šè¿‡ getter è·å–å€¼ï¼Œsetter ç¡®ä¿æ•°æ®çš„åˆæ³•æ€§ã€‚

    - æè¿°ï¼šæœªå®šä¹‰æ„é€ å‡½æ•°æ—¶ï¼ŒJava ç¼–è¯‘å™¨è‡ªåŠ¨æä¾›é»˜è®¤æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ï¼Œå¹¶å¯¹å­—æ®µèµ‹é»˜è®¤å€¼ã€‚å¹¶ä¸ä¼šç›´æ¥æ˜¾å¼çš„åˆ›å»ºåœ¨ä»£ç ä¸­ï¼Œè€Œæ˜¯éšå¼å­˜åœ¨ã€‚

2. è‡ªå®šä¹‰æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ï¼ˆæ¨èå®ç°æ–¹å¼ï¼‰

    ```java
    public class Employee {
        private int baseSalary;
        private int hourlyRate;

        public Employee(int baseSalary, int hourlyRate) {
            setBaseSalary(baseSalary);
            setHourlyRate(hourlyRate);
        }

        public int calculateSalary(int extraHours) {
            return getBaseSalary() + (getHourlyRate() * extraHours);
        }

        public void setBaseSalary(int baseSalary) {
            if (baseSalary <= 0)
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("Base Salary cannot be 0 or less.");
            this.baseSalary = baseSalary;
        }

        private int getBaseSalary() {
            return baseSalary;
        }

        private int getHourlyRate() {
            return hourlyRate;
        }

        public void setHourlyRate(int hourlyRate) {
            if (hourlyRate < 0)
                throw new IllegalArgumentException("Hourly Rate cannot be negative.");
            this.hourlyRate = hourlyRate;
        }
    }
    ```

## ç»ƒä¹ ä»£ç

    ```java
    package com.pang;

    import java.text.NumberFormat;
    import java.util.Scanner;

    public class Main {
      final static byte MONTHS_IN_YEAR = 12;
      final static byte PERCENTAGE = 100;

      public static void main(String[] args) {
          Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

          int principal = (int) readNumber("Principal: ", 1000, 1_000_000);
          float annualInterestRate = (float) readNumber("Annual Interest Rate: ", 1, 30);
          byte periodYear = (byte) readNumber("Period Year: ", 1, 30);

          printMortgage(principal, annualInterestRate, periodYear);
          printPaymentsSchedule(periodYear, principal, annualInterestRate);
      }

      private static void printMortgage(int principal, float annualInterestRate, byte periodYear) {
          double monthlyMortgage = caculateMortgage(principal, annualInterestRate, periodYear);

          String monthlyMortgageFormatted = NumberFormat.getCurrencyInstance().format(monthlyMortgage);
          System.out.println("\nMortgage");
          System.out.println("---------");
          System.out.println("Monthly Payment: " + monthlyMortgageFormatted);
      }

      private static void printPaymentsSchedule(byte periodYear, int principal, float annualInterestRate) {
          System.out.println("\nPayment Schedule");
          System.out.println("----------------");
          for (short month = 1; month <= periodYear * MONTHS_IN_YEAR; month++) {
              double balance = caculateBalance(principal, annualInterestRate, periodYear, month);
              System.out.println(NumberFormat.getCurrencyInstance().format(balance));

          }
      }

      public static double readNumber(String prompt, double min, double max) {
          Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);
          double value;
          while (true) {
              System.out.print(prompt);
              value = scanner.nextFloat();
              if (value >= min && value <= max) break;
              System.out.print("Enter a value between " + min + " and " + max);
          }
          return value;
      }

      public static double caculateMortgage(
              int principal,
              float annualInterestRate,
              byte periodYear) {

          float monthlyInterestRate = annualInterestRate / MONTHS_IN_YEAR / PERCENTAGE;
          int periodMonth = periodYear * MONTHS_IN_YEAR;

          double monthlyMortgage = principal
                  - monthlyInterestRate * Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth)
                  / (Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth) - 1);

          return monthlyMortgage;
      }

      public static double caculateBalance(
              int principal,
              float annualInterestRate,
              byte periodYear,
              short paymentsMade) {

          float monthlyInterestRate = annualInterestRate / MONTHS_IN_YEAR / PERCENTAGE;
          int periodMonth = periodYear * MONTHS_IN_YEAR;

          double banlance = principal *
                  (Math.pow((1 + monthlyInterestRate), periodMonth)
                          - Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, paymentsMade))
                  / (Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth) - 1);

          return banlance;
      }
    }
    ```

## ä¿®æ”¹æ€è·¯

**ä¿®æ”¹æ€è·¯**

1. å­˜åœ¨å‡ ä¸ªæ–¹æ³•ï¼Œå°†å…¶æå–åˆ°æ–°çš„ç±»ä¸­ï¼ˆControl+Tï¼Œå¿«æ·é”®æ“ä½œè§ç½®é¡¶ç« èŠ‚ï¼‰

**ä¿®æ”¹åä»£ç **

- `Console.java`

    ```java
    public class Console {

    	private static Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

    	public static double readNumber(String prompt) {
    		return scanner.nextDouble();
    	}
    	public static double readNumber(String prompt, double min, double max) {
    		double value;
    		while (true) {
    			System.out.print(prompt);
    			value = scanner.nextDouble();
    			if (value >= min && value <= max) break;
    			System.out.print("Enter a value between " + min + " and " + max);
    		}
    		return value;
    	}
    }
    ```

- `MortgageReport.java`

    ```java
    package com.pang;

    import java.text.NumberFormat;

    public class MortgageReport {

        private final NumberFormat currencyInstance;
        private  MortgageCalculate mortgageCalculate;

        public MortgageReport(MortgageCalculate mortgageCalculate) {
            this.mortgageCalculate = mortgageCalculate;
            currencyInstance = NumberFormat.getCurrencyInstance();
        }

        public void printMortgage() {
            double monthlyMortgage = mortgageCalculate.caculateMortgage();

            String monthlyMortgageFormatted = currencyInstance.format(monthlyMortgage);
            System.out.println("\nMortgage");
            System.out.println("---------");
            System.out.println("Monthly Payment: " + monthlyMortgageFormatted);
        }

        public void printPaymentsSchedule() {
            System.out.println("\nPayment Schedule");
            System.out.println("----------------");
            for(double balance : mortgageCalculate.getRemainingBanlance())
                System.out.println(currencyInstance.format(balance));
        }
    }
    ```

- `MortgageCalculate.java`

    ```java
    package com.pang;

    public class MortgageCalculate {

        private final static byte MONTHS_IN_YEAR = 12;
        private final static byte PERCENTAGE = 100;
        private int principal;
        private float annualInterestRate;
        private byte periodYear;

        public MortgageCalculate(int principal, float annualInterestRate, byte periodYear) {
            this.principal = principal;
            this.annualInterestRate = annualInterestRate;
            this.periodYear = periodYear;
        }

        public  double caculateMortgage() {

            float monthlyInterestRate = getMonthlyInterestRate();
            int periodMonth = getPeriodMonth();

            double monthlyMortgage = principal
                    - monthlyInterestRate * Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth)
                    / (Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth) - 1);

            return monthlyMortgage;
        }

        public  double caculateBalance(
                short paymentsMade) {

            float monthlyInterestRate = getMonthlyInterestRate();
            int periodMonth = getPeriodMonth();

            double banlance = principal *
                    (Math.pow((1 + monthlyInterestRate), periodMonth)
                            - Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, paymentsMade))
                    / (Math.pow(1 + monthlyInterestRate, periodMonth) - 1);

            return banlance;
        }

        public double[] getRemainingBanlance() {
            var balances = new double[getPeriodMonth()];
            for (short month = 1; month <= balances.length * MortgageCalculate.MONTHS_IN_YEAR; month++) {
                balances[month - 1] = caculateBalance(month);
            }
            return balances;
        }

        private int getPeriodMonth() {
            int periodMonth = periodYear * MONTHS_IN_YEAR;
            return periodMonth;
        }

        private float getMonthlyInterestRate() {
            float monthlyInterestRate = annualInterestRate / MONTHS_IN_YEAR / PERCENTAGE;
            return monthlyInterestRate;
        }
    }
    ```

- `Main.java`

    ```java
    package com.pang;

    import java.util.Scanner;

    public class Main {

        public static void main(String[] args) {
            Scanner scanner = new Scanner(System.in);

            int principal = (int) Console.readNumber("Principal: ", 1000, 1_000_000);
            float annualInterestRate = (float) Console.readNumber("Annual Interest Rate: ", 1, 30);
            byte periodYear = (byte) Console.readNumber("Period Year: ", 1, 30);

            var mortgageCalculate = new MortgageCalculate(principal, annualInterestRate, periodYear);
            var mortgageReport = new MortgageReport(mortgageCalculate);

            mortgageReport.printMortgage();
            mortgageReport.printPaymentsSchedule();
        }

    }
    ```

    ```java
    public class Main {
    ```

## æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ç»§æ‰¿

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šæ„é€ å‡½æ•°åœ¨å¯¹è±¡åˆ›å»ºæ—¶è‡ªåŠ¨è°ƒç”¨ï¼Œå­ç±»æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ä¼šè‡ªåŠ¨è°ƒç”¨çˆ¶ç±»æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ã€‚è‹¥çˆ¶æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ä¸­å­˜åœ¨å‚æ•°ï¼Œéœ€è¦åœ¨å­æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ä¸­ä½¿ç”¨ super() è¿›è¡Œç»§æ‰¿ã€‚

**çŸ¥è¯†æ ‘**

1. æ„é€ å‡½æ•°åŸºç¡€

    - å®šä¹‰ï¼šä¸ç±»åŒåã€æ— è¿”å›ç±»å‹çš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œåœ¨åˆ›å»ºå¯¹è±¡æ—¶è‡ªåŠ¨è°ƒç”¨
    - ä½œç”¨ï¼šåˆå§‹åŒ–ç±»å®ä¾‹ï¼Œç¡®ä¿å¯¹è±¡çŠ¶æ€æœ‰æ•ˆã€‚
    - é»˜è®¤æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ï¼šè‹¥æœªæ˜¾å¼å®šä¹‰æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ï¼Œç¼–è¯‘å™¨è‡ªåŠ¨ç”Ÿæˆæ— å‚é»˜è®¤æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ã€‚
    - è‡ªå®šä¹‰æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ï¼šä¸€æ—¦å®šä¹‰å¸¦å‚æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ï¼Œé»˜è®¤æ— å‚æ„é€ å‡½æ•°å°†å¤±æ•ˆï¼Œéœ€æ˜¾å¼é‡æ–°å®šä¹‰ã€‚

2. ç»§æ‰¿ä¸­çš„æ„é€ å‡½æ•°è°ƒç”¨

    - è‡ªåŠ¨è°ƒç”¨ï¼šå­ç±»æ„é€ å‡½æ•°é»˜è®¤éšå¼è°ƒç”¨çˆ¶ç±»çš„æ— å‚æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ã€‚

        - `super(...)` è°ƒç”¨å¿…é¡»ä½äºå­ç±»æ„é€ å‡½æ•°çš„ç¬¬ä¸€è¡Œã€‚
    - çˆ¶ç±»åŒæ—¶å®šä¹‰äº†æ— å‚å’Œå¸¦å‚æ•°æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ï¼š
        - å­ç±»é»˜è®¤ç»§æ‰¿æ— å‚æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ï¼›
        - å¦‚éœ€è°ƒç”¨å¸¦å‚æ•°æ„é€ å‡½æ•°ï¼Œå¯æ‰‹åŠ¨ä½¿ç”¨ `super(...)` æŒ‡å®šè°ƒç”¨ã€‚

**ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹**

1. çˆ¶ç±» UIControl ç¤ºä¾‹

    ```java
    public class UIControl {
        // å°è£…æ§ä»¶çŠ¶æ€ï¼Œé»˜è®¤å¯ç”¨
        private boolean isEnabled = true;

        public UIControl() {
            System.out.println("UIControl with no parameters");
        }

        public UIControl(boolean isEnabled) {
            this.isEnabled = isEnabled;
            System.out.println("UIControl with parameter");
        }

        // å¯ç”¨æ§ä»¶
        public void enable() {
            isEnabled = true;
        }

        // ç¦ç”¨æ§ä»¶
        public void disable() {
            isEnabled = false;
        }

        // è¿”å›æ§ä»¶çŠ¶æ€
        public boolean isEnabled() {
            return isEnabled;
        }
    }
    ```

2. å­ç±» TextBox è°ƒç”¨çˆ¶ç±»æ„é€ å‡½æ•°

    ```java
    // ä½¿ç”¨ extend å…³é”®å­—å®ç°ç»§æ‰¿
    public class TextBox extends UIControl {
        public TextBox() {
            super(true); // ä½¿ç”¨superåè°ƒç”¨çˆ¶ç±»å¸¦å‚æ„é€ å‡½æ•°
            System.out.println("TextBox");
        }

        private String text = ""; // Field

        public void setText(String text) {
            this.text = text;
        }

        public void clear() {
            this.text = "";
        }
    }
    ```

3. Main.java

    ```java

        public static void main(String[] args) {
            var box1 = new TextBox();
        }
    }
    ```

1.  é‡å†™ toString() æ–¹æ³•ç¤ºä¾‹

    ```java
    public class TextBox extends UIControl {

        private String text = ""; // Field

        public void setText(String text) {
            this.text = text;
        }

        public void clear() {
            this.text = "";
        }

        public String toString() {
            return "TextBox{" +
                    "text='" + text + '\'' +
                    '}';
        }
    }
    ```

## å‘ä¸Šè½¬å‹ä¸å‘ä¸‹è½¬å‹

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šå‘ä¸Šè½¬å‹ï¼ˆUpcastingï¼‰æŒ‡å­ç±»å¯¹è±¡è½¬æ¢ä¸ºçˆ¶ç±»ç±»å‹ï¼Œå®‰å…¨ä¸”è‡ªåŠ¨å®Œæˆï¼›å‘ä¸‹è½¬å‹ï¼ˆDowncastingï¼‰æŒ‡çˆ¶ç±»å¼•ç”¨è½¬æ¢å›å­ç±»ç±»å‹ï¼Œéœ€æ˜¾å¼è½¬æ¢ï¼Œå­˜åœ¨ç±»å‹å®‰å…¨é£é™©ï¼Œåº”ç»“åˆ instanceof å…³é”®å­—è¿›è¡Œåˆ¤æ–­ã€‚

        - å»ºè®®ç»“åˆ `instanceof` è¿›è¡Œå®‰å…¨æ£€æŸ¥

3. ä½¿ç”¨ `instanceof` å…³é”®å­—è¿›è¡Œç±»å‹æ£€æŸ¥

    - ä½œç”¨ï¼šé¿å…å‘ä¸‹è½¬å‹æ—¶çš„ç±»å‹è½¬æ¢å¼‚å¸¸

## å‘ä¸Šè½¬å‹ä¸å‘ä¸‹è½¬å‹ï¼ˆUpcasting & Downcastingï¼‰

> ç®€è¿°ï¼šå‘ä¸Šè½¬å‹æŒ‡å­ç±»å¯¹è±¡è‡ªåŠ¨è½¬æ¢ä¸ºçˆ¶ç±»å¼•ç”¨ï¼Œå®‰å…¨ä¸”éšå¼å®Œæˆï¼›å‘ä¸‹è½¬å‹æŒ‡çˆ¶ç±»å¼•ç”¨å¼ºåˆ¶è½¬æ¢ä¸ºå­ç±»å¼•ç”¨ï¼Œéœ€æ˜¾å¼å£°æ˜ï¼Œå­˜åœ¨ç±»å‹å®‰å…¨é£é™©ï¼Œéœ€è°¨æ…ä½¿ç”¨ã€‚

**çŸ¥è¯†æ ‘**

1. å‘ä¸Šè½¬å‹ï¼ˆUpcastingï¼‰

    - å­ç±»å¯¹è±¡è‡ªåŠ¨èµ‹ç»™çˆ¶ç±»å¼•ç”¨ï¼ˆéšå¼ï¼‰
    - å®‰å…¨ï¼šå­ç±»å¿…å®šåŒ…å«çˆ¶ç±»æ‰€æœ‰ç‰¹æ€§ï¼Œç¬¦åˆã€Œis-aã€å…³ç³»

2. å‘ä¸‹è½¬å‹ï¼ˆDowncastingï¼‰

    - çˆ¶ç±»å¼•ç”¨æ˜¾å¼å¼ºè½¬ä¸ºå­ç±»å¼•ç”¨ï¼ˆæ˜¾å¼ï¼‰
    - é£é™©ï¼šè‹¥çˆ¶ç±»å¼•ç”¨å®é™…éå­ç±»å®ä¾‹ï¼Œå°†è§¦å‘`ClassCastException`å¼‚å¸¸
    - å‰ç½®æ¡ä»¶ï¼šç¡®ä¿çˆ¶ç±»å¼•ç”¨å®é™…æŒ‡å‘å­ç±»å®ä¾‹ï¼Œå¯å€ŸåŠ©`instanceof`åˆ¤æ–­

3. `instanceof`å…³é”®å­—

    - åŠŸèƒ½ï¼šè¿è¡Œæ—¶æ£€æŸ¥å¯¹è±¡çœŸå®ç±»å‹
    - ç›®çš„ï¼šåœ¨è¿›è¡Œå‘ä¸‹è½¬å‹å‰ç¡®ä¿å®‰å…¨ï¼Œé¿å…å¼ºåˆ¶è½¬æ¢å¼‚å¸¸

4. è½¬å‹çš„è®¾è®¡åŸåˆ™
    - å°½é‡é¿å…é¢‘ç¹ä½¿ç”¨å‘ä¸‹è½¬å‹ï¼Œä»¥å¤šæ€è®¾è®¡å–è€Œä»£ä¹‹
    - è°¨æ…è¿›è¡Œå¼ºåˆ¶ç±»å‹è½¬æ¢ï¼Œç¡®ä¿ç±»å‹å®‰å…¨ï¼Œé¿å…è¿è¡Œæ—¶å¼‚å¸¸

**ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹**

1. å‘ä¸Šè½¬å‹ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼ˆå®‰å…¨ã€è‡ªåŠ¨ï¼‰


2. å‘ä¸‹è½¬å‹ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼ˆæ˜¾å¼ã€æœ‰é£é™©ï¼‰

    - æè¿°ï¼šçˆ¶ç±»å®ä¾‹å¼ºåˆ¶è½¬å‹ä¸ºå­ç±»å®ä¾‹ï¼Œè¿è¡Œæ—¶å‡ºç°å¼‚å¸¸ã€‚

3. ä½¿ç”¨`instanceof`å®‰å…¨å‘ä¸‹è½¬å‹

    ```java

            TextBox textBox = (TextBox) control; // å®‰å…¨è½¬å‹

    public static void main(String[] args) {
    ```

    - æè¿°ï¼šåˆ©ç”¨`instanceof`ç¡®ä¿ç±»å‹å®‰å…¨åï¼Œå†æ‰§è¡Œå‘ä¸‹è½¬å‹ï¼Œé¿å…å‡ºç°`ClassCastException`å¼‚å¸¸ã€‚
